</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to react [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(to)</span></span>], to capitalise [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(on)</span></span>] <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to respond to certain circumstances with action or behaviour</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***instantie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:instantie.html>instantie</a> (13181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">instance</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">instantia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a being near, presence, also perseverance, earnestness, importunity, urgency</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">instans</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">urgent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See instant.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:instantie.html>instantie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:instanties.html>instanties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:instantie.html>instantietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>authority</li>
<li>agency, <a href = vnd.unilang:bureau.html>bureau</a></li>
<li>instance <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only in limited contexts</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:instantie.html>instantie</a></b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">In the first <b>instance</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***instemmen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:instemmen.html>instemmen</a> (17343)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stemmen.html>stemmen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to vote, tune</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">einstimmen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:instemmen.html>instemmen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to agree <span class="defdate">[from 17th c.]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:instemming.html>instemming</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:instemmen.html>instemmen</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:instorting.html>instorting</a> (24186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The root of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:instorten.html>instorten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to collapse, implode, inspire etc</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:instorting.html>instorting</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:instortingen.html>instortingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:instorting.html>instortinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A collapse, implosion etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A breakdown, downfall, undoing; decay; grave medical relapse</li>

<li>An infusion</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:interessant.html>interessant</a> (1120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">intéressant</i>, present participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">intéresser</i>.

</p>

<li>notable, important</li>
<li>profitable, benefic</li></ol>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">interfere</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-on</i>, from its role interfering with viral replication.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:interferon.html>interferon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">interferons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biochemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of a group of glycoproteins, produced by the immune system, that prevent viral replication in infected cells.</li></ol>

***internationaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:internationaal.html>internationaal</a> (8202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">international</i>, apparently coined in 1780 by Jeremy Bentham from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">inter-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">national</i> (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">inter-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nationaal.html>nationaal</a></i>), both ultimately from Latin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:internationaal.html>internationaal</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:internationaal.html>internationaler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">internationaalst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>international, between, concerning, or transcending multiple nations</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">international</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:internationaal.html>internationaal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:internationaal.html>internationalen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:internationaal.html>internationaaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An international actor, e.g. player in a national sports team</li>
<li>A stock that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> traded on exchanges in different countries</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">international</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:internationaal.html>internationaal</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:internationaal.html>internationaal</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> één <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:betrokken.html>betrokken</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:vertegenwoordigd.html>vertegenwoordigd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:internationaal.html>internationaal</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdrag.html>verdrag</a>.</i> </li>
